Introduction

Base URL: http://mypeltar

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

To authenticate requests, include an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Assets

Display a listing of the resource.

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/getall" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/getall"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/getall',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
import requests
import json

url = 'http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/getall'
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('GET', url, headers=headers)
response.json()

GET api/v1/asset/search

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/search" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/search"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/search',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',

Store a newly created resource in storage.

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/store" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"stockcode\": \"expedita\",
    \"serialnumber\": \"culpa\",
    \"nama_asset\": \"asjwvvumpuwhwameizafjwfylttensgtlqjhhnyimdcsinqlbczcadc\",
    \"merk\": \"maxime\",
    \"model\": \"officiis\",
    \"spesifikasi\": \"odit\",
    \"deskripsi\": \"amet\",
    \"id_lokasi\": 16,
    \"id_status\": 6
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/store"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "stockcode": "expedita",
    "serialnumber": "culpa",
    "nama_asset": "asjwvvumpuwhwameizafjwfylttensgtlqjhhnyimdcsinqlbczcadc",
    "merk": "maxime",
    "model": "officiis",
    "spesifikasi": "odit",
    "deskripsi": "amet",
    "id_lokasi": 16,
    "id_status": 6
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/store',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'stockcode' => 'expedita',
            'serialnumber' => 'culpa',
            'nama_asset' => 'asjwvvumpuwhwameizafjwfylttensgtlqjhhnyimdcsinqlbczcadc',
            'merk' => 'maxime',
            'model' => 'officiis',
            'spesifikasi' => 'odit',
            'deskripsi' => 'amet',
            'id_lokasi' => 16,
            'id_status' => 6,
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
import requests
import json

url = 'http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/store'
payload = {
    "stockcode": "expedita",
    "serialnumber": "culpa",
    "nama_asset": "asjwvvumpuwhwameizafjwfylttensgtlqjhhnyimdcsinqlbczcadc",
    "merk": "maxime",
    "model": "officiis",
    "spesifikasi": "odit",
    "deskripsi": "amet",
    "id_lokasi": 16,
    "id_status": 6
}
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('POST', url, headers=headers, json=payload)
response.json()

Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/v1/asset/store

Headers

Authorization      

Example: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

stockcode   string   

Example: expedita

serialnumber   string   

Example: culpa

nama_asset   string  optional  

Must be at least 6 characters. Example: asjwvvumpuwhwameizafjwfylttensgtlqjhhnyimdcsinqlbczcadc

merk   string   

Example: maxime

model   string  optional  

Example: officiis

spesifikasi   string  optional  

Example: odit

deskripsi   string  optional  

Example: amet

id_lokasi   integer   

Example: 16

id_kategori   object  optional  
id_status   integer   

Example: 6

Display the specified resource.

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/show/1" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/show/1"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/show/1',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

import json

url = 'http://mypeltar/api/v1/asset/show/1'
